info:8 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted October 3, 2023
msg:The first time I stayed here was to watch the event, and then I found that there were still some places to go in Beilun, so I chose Dongqian Lake + Beilun for the National Day holiday. The hotel room is nice, the location is good, and it is convenient for self-driving tours. There is also a subway across the intersection. There are stalls and street singers in the festival at Fubon Plaza across the road, full of fireworks.
There are Jiufeng Mountain to climb around, and Beilun Fuquan Mountain where Internet celebrities watch the sunrise. It is quite convenient to go to Tiantong Temple or Dongqian Lake. The small regret is that there are not many delicious restaurants around.
I brought a carry-on suitcase, and there are three or four steps from the hotel entrance to the front desk. There is no waiter to help, and there is no ramp to pull the suitcase, so I have to carry the suitcase up the steps. Maybe the hotel needs to think from the perspective of the guests and find a solution to improve the check-in experience.
